        log(`Error processing entity ${entity.name}`, 'error', entityError);\n        }\n      }",
  "new_string": "      log(`Persisting ${entities.length} entities for team: ${team}`, 'info');\n\n      // Process entities in parallel batches for performance\n      const CONCURRENCY = 10; // Process 10 entities concurrently\n      const validEntities = entities.filter(e => e.name && e.name.trim() !== '');\n      const skippedCount = entities.length - validEntities.length;\n      if (skippedCount > 0) {\n        log(`Skipping ${skippedCount} entities with empty names`, 'warning');\n        result.failed += skippedCount;\n      }\n\n      // Helper to process a single entity\n      const processEntity = async (entity: typeof entities[0]): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'failed'> => {\n        try {\n          // Check if entity already exists\n          const existingEntity = await this.getEntity(entity.name, team);\n\n          if (existingEntity) {\n            // Update existing entity - add new observations\n            const newObservations = entity.observations.filter(\n              obs => !existingEntity.observations.some(\n                existing => (typeof existing === 'string' ? existing : existing.content) === obs\n              )\n            );\n\n            if (newObservations.length > 0) {\n              const updateResult = await this.updateEntityObservations({\n                entityName: entity.name,\n                team,\n                removeObservations: [],\n                newObservations\n              });\n\n              if (updateResult.success) {\n                log(`Updated entity: ${entity.name} with ${newObservations.length} new observations`, 'debug');\n                return 'updated';\n              } else {\n                log(`Failed to update entity: ${entity.name}`, 'warning');\n                return 'failed';\n              }\n            } else {\n              // Entity exists but no new observations - count as updated (no-op)\n              return 'updated';\n            }\n          } else {\n            // Create new entity using storeEntityToGraph (direct GraphDB storage)\n            const currentDate = new Date().toISOString();\n            const sharedMemoryEntity: SharedMemoryEntity = {\n              id: `entity_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`,\n              name: entity.name,\n              entityType: entity.entityType,\n              significance: entity.significance || 5,\n              observations: entity.observations.map(obs => {\n                if (typeof obs === 'object' && obs !== null && 'type' in obs && 'content' in obs) {\n                  const typedObs = obs as { type: string; content: string; date?: string; metadata?: Record<string, unknown> };\n                  return {\n                    type: typedObs.type || 'insight',\n                    content: typedObs.content,\n                    date: typedObs.date || currentDate,\n                    metadata: {\n                      ...typedObs.metadata,\n                      source: (typedObs.metadata?.source as string) || 'workflow_persist'\n                    }\n                  };\n                }\n                return {\n                  type: 'insight',\n                  content: String(obs),\n                  date: currentDate,\n                  metadata: { source: 'workflow_persist' }\n                };\n              }),\n              relationships: [],\n              metadata: {\n                created_at: currentDate,\n                last_updated: currentDate,\n                created_by: 'workflow_persist',\n                version: '1.0'\n              }\n            };\n\n            const nodeId = await this.storeEntityToGraph(sharedMemoryEntity);\n            log(`Created entity: ${entity.name} (nodeId: ${nodeId})`, 'debug');\n            return 'created';\n          }\n        } catch (entityError) {\n          log(`Error processing entity ${entity.name}`, 'error', entityError);\n          return 'failed';\n        }\n      };\n\n      // Process in parallel batches\n      const startTime = Date.now();\n      for (let i = 0; i < validEntities.length; i += CONCURRENCY) {\n        const batch = validEntities.slice(i, i + CONCURRENCY);\n        const batchResults = await Promise.all(batch.map(processEntity));\n\n        for (const r of batchResults) {\n          if (r === 'created') result.created++;\n          else if (r === 'updated') result.updated++;\n          else result.failed++;\n        }\n\n        // Progress log every batch\n        const progress = Math.min(100, Math.round(((i + batch.length) / validEntities.length) * 100));\n        log(`Persistence progress: ${progress}% (${i + batch.length}/${validEntities.length})`, 'info');\n      }\n      const elapsed = ((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000).toFixed(1);\n      log(`Persistence completed in ${elapsed}s`, 'info');"
}

   - 2026-01-11 1800-1900: System Health Dashboard workflow visualization
   - Cross-project logs from ui-template

2. **`ukb full` command**: User requested full UKB analysis. I started the `complete-analysis` workflow with workflow ID `wf_1768289265103_vnbbav`.

3. **Dashboard Graph Issue #1**: User reported "you are again on ontology without the graph showing the step as green (and highlighted)". The Ontology node showed "Completed" in sidebar but wasn't green in the graph.
   - **Root Cause**: In `ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`, the `process.currentStep` override at lines 1335-1343 was unconditionally setting status to 'running', overriding completed steps.
   - **Fix**: Added check to NOT override if step is already 'completed' or 'failed'.

4. **Dashboard Graph Issue #2**: User reported "after ontology it didn't highlight KG-Ops... git... and ontology 'orphaned'". When starting new batch, previous batch's completed steps remained green instead of resetting.
   - **Root Cause**: `BATCH_PHASE_STEPS` logic wasn't properly resetting steps when a new batch started.
   - **Fix**: Added `currentBatchStepIndex` tracking to force steps AFTER current position to 'pending' status.

5. **Persistence Timeout Issue**: User reported persistence step taking too long (failed with "Step timeout after 120s").
   - **Root Cause**: `persistEntities` method in `persistence-agent.ts` processed entities sequentially.
   - **Fix**: Parallelized with CONCURRENCY=10, using `Promise.all` with batched processing.
   - Also increased timeout from 120s to 300s in `batch-analysis.yaml`.

6. **Ontology 36-minute Issue**: User asked why ontology classification took 36 minutes and failed.
   - Investigating `OntologyClassifier` and its `classify` method.

7. **Unknown Entities in Output**: User pointed out ontology classification shows "name: unknown, class: unknown" even though classification IS working (byClass shows proper counts).
   - **Root Cause**: In coordinator.ts line 2581-2584, wrong property paths were used:
     - Was: `c.entity?.name` and `c.ontologyClass`
     - Should be: `c.original?.name` and `c.ontologyMetadata?.ontologyClass`
   - **Fix Applied**: Updated the mapping to use correct paths.

8. **KG Operators Lacking Detail**: User wanted to see actual entity names, not just counts.
   - **Fix Applied**: Added entity names and relations to kg_operators tracking output.

9. **Git/Vibe Lacking Detail**: User reported git only shows `commitsCount: 44` and vibe only shows `sessionsCount: 45` - wants actual commit messages and session topics.
   - **Currently Working On**: Need to add commit messages and session details to tracking.

     ```typescript
     // Infer current step from process.currentStep
     // Only override to 'running' if step hasn't already completed/failed (prevents resetting completed steps)
     if (process.currentStep) {
       const currentAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep
       const existingStatus = map[currentAgentId]?.status
       // Don't override completed/failed steps - they should retain their final status
       if (existingStatus !== 'completed' && existingStatus !== 'failed') {
         if (map[currentAgentId]) {
           map[currentAgentId] = { ...map[currentAgentId], status: 'running' }
         } else {
           map[currentAgentId] = { name: process.currentStep, status: 'running' }
         }
       }
     }
     ```
     - Fix 2: Reset future batch steps to pending based on current step position:
     ```typescript
     // Determine current step position in batch sequence to reset future steps
     const currentAgentFromStep = process.currentStep
       ? (STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep)
       : null
     const currentBatchStepIndex = currentAgentFromStep
       ? BATCH_PHASE_STEPS.indexOf(currentAgentFromStep)
       : -1
     
     // If this step comes AFTER the current step in the batch sequence,
     // it hasn't run in this batch yet - force pending
     if (currentBatchStepIndex >= 0 && stepIndex > currentBatchStepIndex) {
       map[agentId] = { ...step, status: 'pending' }
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/persistence-agent.ts`**
     - Parallelized `persistEntities` method (was sequential, causing timeout)
     ```typescript
     // Process entities in parallel batches for performance
     const CONCURRENCY = 10; // Process 10 entities concurrently
     const validEntities = entities.filter(e => e.name && e.name.trim() !== '');
     
     const processEntity = async (entity: typeof entities[0]): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'failed'> => {
       // ... entity processing logic
     };
     
     // Process in parallel batches
     for (let i = 0; i < validEntities.length; i += CONCURRENCY) {
       const batch = validEntities.slice(i, i + CONCURRENCY);
       const batchResults = await Promise.all(batch.map(processEntity));
       // ... aggregate results
     }
     ```

       agent: persistence
       action: persistEntities
       timeout: 300  # 5 minutes (parallelized processing handles large entity sets)
     ```

Analysis:
Let me analyze the conversation chronologically:

1. **Session Start - `/sl` command**: User requested session log reading for continuity. I found we're in the coding project and read recent session logs from:
   - 2026-01-13 0700-0800: Major work on UKB system, VKB orphan node removal issue

   - 2026-01-11 1800-1900: System Health Dashboard workflow visualization
   - Cross-project logs from ui-template

2. **`ukb full` command**: User requested full UKB analysis. I started the `complete-analysis` workflow with workflow ID `wf_1768289265103_vnbbav`.

3. **Dashboard Graph Issue #1**: User reported "you are again on ontology without the graph showing the step as green (and highlighted)". The Ontology node showed "Completed" in sidebar but wasn't green in the graph.
   - **Root Cause**: In `ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`, the `process.currentStep` override at lines 1335-1343 was unconditionally setting status to 'running', overriding completed steps.
   - **Fix**: Added check to NOT override if step is already 'completed' or 'failed'.

4. **Dashboard Graph Issue #2**: User reported "after ontology it didn't highlight KG-Ops... git... and ontology 'orphaned'". When starting new batch, previous batch's completed steps remained green instead of resetting.
   - **Root Cause**: `BATCH_PHASE_STEPS` logic wasn't properly resetting steps when a new batch started.
   - **Fix**: Added `currentBatchStepIndex` tracking to force steps AFTER current position to 'pending' status.

5. **Persistence Timeout Issue**: User reported persistence step taking too long (failed with "Step timeout after 120s").
   - **Root Cause**: `persistEntities` method in `persistence-agent.ts` processed entities sequentially.
   - **Fix**: Parallelized with CONCURRENCY=10, using `Promise.all` with batched processing.
   - Also increased timeout from 120s to 300s in `batch-analysis.yaml`.

6. **Ontology 36-minute Issue**: User asked why ontology classification took 36 minutes and failed.
   - Investigating `OntologyClassifier` and its `classify` method.

7. **Unknown Entities in Output**: User pointed out ontology classification shows "name: unknown, class: unknown" even though classification IS working (byClass shows proper counts).
   - **Root Cause**: In coordinator.ts line 2581-2584, wrong property paths were used:
     - Was: `c.entity?.name` and `c.ontologyClass`
     - Should be: `c.original?.name` and `c.ontologyMetadata?.ontologyClass`
   - **Fix Applied**: Updated the mapping to use correct paths.

8. **KG Operators Lacking Detail**: User wanted to see actual entity names, not just counts.
   - **Fix Applied**: Added entity names and relations to kg_operators tracking output.

9. **Git/Vibe Lacking Detail**: User reported git only shows `commitsCount: 44` and vibe only shows `sessionsCount: 45` - wants actual commit messages and session topics.
   - **Currently Working On**: Need to add commit messages and session details to tracking.

   - System Health Dashboard visualization of workflow progress
   - React useMemo for step status computation
   - BATCH_PHASE_STEPS - steps that repeat each batch and need status reset
   - Parallel entity processing with controlled concurrency
   - ClassifiedObservation structure: `{ original, ontologyMetadata, classified }`
   - Step tracking via `trackBatchStep()` function

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`integrations/system-health-dashboard/src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`**
     - Central file for workflow visualization
     - Fix 1: Prevent overriding completed steps with 'running' status:
     ```typescript
     // Infer current step from process.currentStep
     // Only override to 'running' if step hasn't already completed/failed (prevents resetting completed steps)
     if (process.currentStep) {
       const currentAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep
       const existingStatus = map[currentAgentId]?.status
       // Don't override completed/failed steps - they should retain their final status
       if (existingStatus !== 'completed' && existingStatus !== 'failed') {
         if (map[currentAgentId]) {
           map[currentAgentId] = { ...map[currentAgentId], status: 'running' }
         } else {
           map[currentAgentId] = { name: process.currentStep, status: 'running' }
         }
       }
     }
     ```
     - Fix 2: Reset future batch steps to pending based on current step position:
     ```typescript
     // Determine current step position in batch sequence to reset future steps
     const currentAgentFromStep = process.currentStep
       ? (STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep)
       : null
     const currentBatchStepIndex = currentAgentFromStep
       ? BATCH_PHASE_STEPS.indexOf(currentAgentFromStep)
       : -1
     
     // If this step comes AFTER the current step in the batch sequence,
     // it hasn't run in this batch yet - force pending
     if (currentBatchStepIndex >= 0 && stepIndex > currentBatchStepIndex) {
       map[agentId] = { ...step, status: 'pending' }
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/persistence-agent.ts`**
     - Parallelized `persistEntities` method (was sequential, causing timeout)
     ```typescript
     // Process entities in parallel batches for performance
     const CONCURRENCY = 10; // Process 10 entities concurrently
     const validEntities = entities.filter(e => e.name && e.name.trim() !== '');
     
     const processEntity = async (entity: typeof entities[0]): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'failed'> => {
       // ... entity processing logic
     };
     
     // Process in parallel batches
     for (let i = 0; i < validEntities.length; i += CONCURRENCY) {
       const batch = validEntities.slice(i, i + CONCURRENCY);
       const batchResults = await Promise.all(batch.map(processEntity));
       // ... aggregate results
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/config/workflows/batch-analysis.yaml`**
     - Increased `final_persist` timeout from 120s to 300s
     ```yaml
     - name: final_persist
       agent: persistence
       action: persistEntities
       timeout: 300  # 5 minutes (parallelized processing handles large entity sets)
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/coordinator.ts`**
     - Fixed classifiedEntities mapping (was using wrong property paths):
     ```typescript
     classifiedEntities: classifiedEntities.slice(0, 5).map((c: any) => ({
       name: c.original?.name || c.original?.entityName || c.name || 'unknown',
       class: c.ontologyMetadata?.ontologyClass || c.ontologyClass || 'unknown'
     }))
     ```
     - Enhanced kg_operators tracking with entity names:
     ```typescript
     trackBatchStep('kg_operators', 'completed', operatorsTotalDuration, {
       entitiesAfter: entityList.length,
       relationsAfter: relationList.length,
       entities: entityList.slice(0, 8).map((e: any) => ({
         name: e.name || e.entity_name || 'unknown',
         type: e.entityType || e.entity_type || e.type || 'Entity'
       })),
       relations: relationList.slice(0, 5).map((r: any) => ({
         from: r.from || r.source,
         to: r.to || r.target,
         type: r.relationType || r.type || 'related_to'
       }))
     });
     ```

3. **Dashboard Graph Issue #1**: User reported "you are again on ontology without the graph showing the step as green (and highlighted)". The Ontology node showed "Completed" in sidebar but wasn't green in the graph.
   - **Root Cause**: In `ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`, the `process.currentStep` override at lines 1335-1343 was unconditionally setting status to 'running', overriding completed steps.
   - **Fix**: Added check to NOT override if step is already 'completed' or 'failed'.

4. **Dashboard Graph Issue #2**: User reported "after ontology it didn't highlight KG-Ops... git... and ontology 'orphaned'". When starting new batch, previous batch's completed steps remained green instead of resetting.
   - **Root Cause**: `BATCH_PHASE_STEPS` logic wasn't properly resetting steps when a new batch started.
   - **Fix**: Added `currentBatchStepIndex` tracking to force steps AFTER current position to 'pending' status.

5. **Persistence Timeout Issue**: User reported persistence step taking too long (failed with "Step timeout after 120s").
   - **Root Cause**: `persistEntities` method in `persistence-agent.ts` processed entities sequentially.
   - **Fix**: Parallelized with CONCURRENCY=10, using `Promise.all` with batched processing.
   - Also increased timeout from 120s to 300s in `batch-analysis.yaml`.

6. **Ontology 36-minute Issue**: User asked why ontology classification took 36 minutes and failed.
   - Investigating `OntologyClassifier` and its `classify` method.

7. **Unknown Entities in Output**: User pointed out ontology classification shows "name: unknown, class: unknown" even though classification IS working (byClass shows proper counts).
   - **Root Cause**: In coordinator.ts line 2581-2584, wrong property paths were used:
     - Was: `c.entity?.name` and `c.ontologyClass`
     - Should be: `c.original?.name` and `c.ontologyMetadata?.ontologyClass`
   - **Fix Applied**: Updated the mapping to use correct paths.

8. **KG Operators Lacking Detail**: User wanted to see actual entity names, not just counts.
   - **Fix Applied**: Added entity names and relations to kg_operators tracking output.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - UKB (Update Knowledge Base) workflow system with batch processing
   - System Health Dashboard visualization of workflow progress
   - React useMemo for step status computation
   - BATCH_PHASE_STEPS - steps that repeat each batch and need status reset
   - Parallel entity processing with controlled concurrency
   - ClassifiedObservation structure: `{ original, ontologyMetadata, classified }`
   - Step tracking via `trackBatchStep()` function

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`integrations/system-health-dashboard/src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`**
     - Central file for workflow visualization
     - Fix 1: Prevent overriding completed steps with 'running' status:
     ```typescript
     // Infer current step from process.currentStep
     // Only override to 'running' if step hasn't already completed/failed (prevents resetting completed steps)
     if (process.currentStep) {
       const currentAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep
       const existingStatus = map[currentAgentId]?.status
       // Don't override completed/failed steps - they should retain their final status
       if (existingStatus !== 'completed' && existingStatus !== 'failed') {
         if (map[currentAgentId]) {
           map[currentAgentId] = { ...map[currentAgentId], status: 'running' }
         } else {
           map[currentAgentId] = { name: process.currentStep, status: 'running' }
         }
       }
     }
     ```
     - Fix 2: Reset future batch steps to pending based on current step position:
     ```typescript
     // Determine current step position in batch sequence to reset future steps
     const currentAgentFromStep = process.currentStep
       ? (STEP_TO_AGENT[process.currentStep] || process.currentStep)
       : null
     const currentBatchStepIndex = currentAgentFromStep
       ? BATCH_PHASE_STEPS.indexOf(currentAgentFromStep)
       : -1
     
     // If this step comes AFTER the current step in the batch sequence,
     // it hasn't run in this batch yet - force pending
     if (currentBatchStepIndex >= 0 && stepIndex > currentBatchStepIndex) {
       map[agentId] = { ...step, status: 'pending' }
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/persistence-agent.ts`**
     - Parallelized `persistEntities` method (was sequential, causing timeout)
     ```typescript
     // Process entities in parallel batches for performance
     const CONCURRENCY = 10; // Process 10 entities concurrently
     const validEntities = entities.filter(e => e.name && e.name.trim() !== '');
     
     const processEntity = async (entity: typeof entities[0]): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'failed'> => {
       // ... entity processing logic
     };
     
     // Process in parallel batches
     for (let i = 0; i < validEntities.length; i += CONCURRENCY) {
       const batch = validEntities.slice(i, i + CONCURRENCY);
       const batchResults = await Promise.all(batch.map(processEntity));
       // ... aggregate results
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/config/workflows/batch-analysis.yaml`**
     - Increased `final_persist` timeout from 120s to 300s
     ```yaml
     - name: final_persist
       agent: persistence
       action: persistEntities
       timeout: 300  # 5 minutes (parallelized processing handles large entity sets)
     ```

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/coordinator.ts`**
     - Fixed classifiedEntities mapping (was using wrong property paths):
     ```typescript
     classifiedEntities: classifiedEntities.slice(0, 5).map((c: any) => ({
       name: c.original?.name || c.original?.entityName || c.name || 'unknown',
       class: c.ontologyMetadata?.ontologyClass || c.ontologyClass || 'unknown'
     }))
     ```
     - Enhanced kg_operators tracking with entity names:
     ```typescript
     trackBatchStep('kg_operators', 'completed', operatorsTotalDuration, {
       entitiesAfter: entityList.length,
       relationsAfter: relationList.length,
       entities: entityList.slice(0, 8).map((e: any) => ({
         name: e.name || e.entity_name || 'unknown',
         type: e.entityType || e.entity_type || e.type || 'Entity'
       })),
       relations: relationList.slice(0, 5).map((r: any) => ({
         from: r.from || r.source,
         to: r.to || r.target,
         type: r.relationType || r.type || 'related_to'
       }))
     });
     ```

2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/2026-01-13_0900-1000_g9b30a.md"
}
```

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "pwd",
  "description": "Get current working directory"
}
```

**Result:** ‚úÖ Success
**Output:** ```
/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding
```
